10. How did the Treaty of Paris connect the Spanish-American War to the Philippine-American War?
11. Why did Jose Rizal become the Supremo of the Katipunan?

13. When is rizal's birthday?

Flow per question:
1. Query analyzer
2. Semantic search
3. BM25 search
4. RRF combine
5. Metadata boost
6. Rerank
7. Final context filter

Any person who wished to join the Katipunan was subjected to certain initiation rites, resembling those of Masonic rites, to test his courage, patriotism and loyalty. New recruits underwent the initiation rite three at a time so that no member knew more than two other members of the society. Katipunan soon gained influence across the islands, and sought an armed revolution. However, that revolution started prematurely in August 1896 upon its discovery by Spanish authorities in Manila.
